<task>
/orchestrator Run Phase 5 from 'docs/phase-plan.md' (see below for file content) as a single Bob session.
Honor every spec field as a binding contract; verify Preconditions before
SPEC and refuse an incomplete or ambiguous spec. Run the encoded loop
(specâ†’implementâ†’reviewâ†’testâ†’fixâ†’enhance) enforcing that phase's named Quality
gates as hard pass/fail and executing the FULL must-test list on the first
pass. Loop is value-gated and conditionally scoped, no iteration cap: a clean
first pass (all AC green, zero reviewer blockers, full must-test green) exits
straight to export â€” skip FIX and ENHANCE, run no re-verification loop; an
unmet criterion gets a scoped FIX plus re-verification of only the affected
criteria and changed-file tests, widening to a full REVIEW+TEST re-run only
on a shared/core contract change. Escalate the precise gap only if two
consecutive loops produce no measurable progress or an external decision is
required. When
acceptance criteria are green with zero reviewer blockers, and delegate the build-report.md row to reviewer,
then STOP for my approval before commit. Never commit autonomously.
</task>

108 | **Acceptance criteria** (binary, testable)
109 | 1. **AC #0 (gating):** Monorepo root manifest exists and parses: `package.json` (name, workspaces, scripts including `test`), `pnpm-workspace.yaml` (packages glob), `tsconfig.base.json` + `tsconfig.json`, `vitest.config.ts`. 111 | 3. `packages/core/discovery.ts` exports a pure function: input `IdeaBrief` (with ecosystem, domain, capabilities); output `string[]` (candidate package names). No I/O, no LLM calls. **Catalog is a static map committed to git in the module or as `fixtures/discovery-catalog.json`.**
112 | 4. `packages/core/scorer.ts` exports a pure function: input `Candidate[]`, `IdeaBrief`, optional `RepoStack`; output `Recommendation[]` with per-dimension subscores (goal fit 30%, repo compat 25%, maintenance 15%, safety 15%, community 10%, docs 5%). Every subscore independently computable from visible inputs. No I/O.
113 | 5. `packages/core/normalizer.ts` exports a function returning `CanonicalId` (npm lowercase, PyPI dash/underscore-normalized, GitHub `owner/repo` lowercase) â€” stable cache key.
114 | 6. `packages/core/serializer.ts` emits missing fields as explicit `null`, rejects silently-omitted evidence.
115 | 7. **Determinism test passes:** scorer + serializer produce byte-identical JSON output across 10 runs when given the same frozen `IdeaBrief` + `Candidate[]` fixture (no LLM stage). Determinism boundary: scorer and serializer only; intent parsing (LLM, in CLI) is excluded from this test. Failure is a BLOCKER.
116 | 8. **Evidence test passes:** missing signal (e.g., no OpenSSF score) does not crash; field is `null` and labeled `(not available)` in output.

146 | 4. **Inference labeling:** `IdeaBrief.capabilities` field has JSDoc `@source: 'inferred'`; serialized output includes source metadata.

152 | **Integration success** â€” P1 outputs pure TypeScript modules (`packages/core/`) with zero I/O: discovery is a static catalog, scoring is pure logic. P2 (collectors) will import types. P3 (CLI) will add the Claude Haiku intent-parsing adapter (the only LLM call, outside core), invoke discovery, fetch evidence via collectors, and score. P5 (web) will import via the CLI bridge. The one-pipeline contract ([`docs/architecture.md`](../docs/architecture.md) Â§13.2) is satisfied: core has zero I/O, so web/skill/CI all call the same logic path through the CLI.

154 | **Loop config**
155 | - **Steps:** SPEC (plan) â†’ IMPLEMENT (code) â†’ REVIEW (reviewer: `code-review`, `evidence-discipline`) â†’ TEST (advanced: `test-runner`, `evidence-discipline`) â†’ FIX (code, conditional) â†’ ENHANCE (code, conditional) â†’ LOOP GATE (value-gated, conditional â€” clean pass exits to EXPORT; unmet â‡’ scoped re-verify) â†’ EXPORT â†’ HUMAN REVIEW â†’ COMMIT (code, Bob-generated message).
156 | - **Delegated mode per step:** SPECâ†’`plan` (no skills; rules-plan) Â· IMPLEMENTâ†’`code` (no skills; rules-code) Â· REVIEWâ†’`reviewer` (`code-review`, `evidence-discipline` skills where supported; always-on rules + rules-reviewer) Â· TESTâ†’`advanced` (`test-runner`, `evidence-discipline` skills; always-on rules) Â· FIXâ†’`code` Â· ENHANCEâ†’`code` Â· COMMITâ†’`code`.
157 | - **Loop continuation:** no fixed iteration cap, conditionally scoped. The first REVIEW+TEST pass is full (full review + full must-test list). A clean pass â€” every acceptance criterion green, zero reviewer blockers, full must-test green â€” exits straight to EXPORT with FIX and ENHANCE skipped; no re-verification loop runs. An unmet criterion triggers a scoped FIX and re-verification of only the affected criteria + changed-file tests (plus a regression sanity), widening to a full REVIEW+TEST re-run only when a shared/core contract (types, scorer, serializer, CLI boundary, public schema) was touched. Each loop names its measurable delta; escalate only if progress stalls for two consecutive loops or an external decision is required.
158 | - **Human gate:** STEP 9 mandatory approval before STEP 10 commit. Never commit autonomously.

169 | ## Phase P2 â€” Collectors + Cache (maps to session S04)
170 | 
171 | **Objective** â€” Establish the single source of factual truth by implementing live collectors for npm and GitHub registries with a transparent local cache, explicit TTLs, and graceful degradation to cached data on rate limits, ensuring every package fact is sourced and timestamped.
172 | 
173 | **Correlation & success measure** â€” This phase directly satisfies [`docs/architecture.md`](../docs/architecture.md) Â§17 judge success criterion #2 ("no hallucination â€” every fact is sourced; every inference is labeled"). Success is measured by: real npm + GitHub data returned live or from cache with explicit `source` labels; cache-fallback test passing; missing evidence (404, unavailable) handled explicitly as `null` with `(not available)` labels; no invented package facts.
174 | 
175 | **Self-contained context** â€” Inputs required:
176 | - [`docs/architecture.md`](../docs/architecture.md) Â§11 (collectors and cache strategy: endpoints, TTLs, error handling, cache schema `{data, collectedAt, source}`), Â§12 (hallucination controls), Â§14 (error handling table)
177 | - [`docs/implementation-plan.md`](../docs/implementation-plan.md) Â§5 P2 (files, notes, tests, exit gate, pro tips)
178 | - P1 output: `packages/core/types.ts` (to type collector responses)
179 | - [`.bob/custom_modes.yaml`](../.bob/custom_modes.yaml) `code` mode `fileRegex` (permits `packages/`)
180 | - [`.bob/rules/01-evidence-discipline.md`](../.bob/rules/01-evidence-discipline.md), [`.bob/rules/02-engineering-standards.md`](../.bob/rules/02-engineering-standards.md)
181 | 
182 | **Scope**
183 | - **In:** `packages/collectors/` with `index.ts` (registry: ecosystem â†’ collector), `npm.ts`, `github.ts`, `cache/index.ts`; unit tests per collector with mocked fetch validated against real response shapes; cache-invalidation tests; error-path tests (404, rate limit, timeout); cache-fallback test; **committed demo fixtures in `fixtures/demo-packages/` (discord.js, discord.py, starter repo metadata snapshots for demo insurance, committed to git).**
184 | - **Out (cutline):** PyPI collector (optional, non-blocking; see should/cut), OpenSSF collector (optional, non-blocking; see should/cut), Hugging Face collector (cut first if behind), live repo analysis, GitHub starter search, web UI, CLI integration (P3), scaffold (P4).
185 | - **Should/cut:** `pypi.ts` and `openssf.ts` are optional, non-blocking acceptance criteria with explicit fixture-fallback degradation paths and hard time-boxes (1 hour each). If time-box expires, degrade to fixture data and mark as cached. P2's blocking exit gate remains npm + GitHub live only.
186 | 
187 | **Preconditions** â€” P1 complete and committed: `packages/core/types.ts` exists and exports `Candidate`, `EvidencePassport` schemas; `pnpm test` in `packages/core/` is green.
188 | 
189 | **Acceptance criteria** (binary, testable)
190 | 1. `packages/collectors/index.ts` exports a registry mapping ecosystem (`'npm'|'pypi'|'github'`) to collector function.
191 | 2. `packages/collectors/npm.ts` exports a function accepting package name, returning `Promise<NpmMetadata>` or throwing `PackageNotFoundError` on 404. Uses `registry.npmjs.org/{name}/latest`. Never returns null or fake data on 404.
192 | 3. `packages/collectors/github.ts` exports a function accepting `owner/repo`, returning `Promise<GitHubMetadata>` or throwing on error. Uses GitHub REST `/repos/{owner}/{repo}` + `/contributors`. On rate limit, returns cached data with `source: 'cache-fallback'` if cache exists; otherwise throws.
193 | 4. `packages/collectors/cache/index.ts` stores `{data, collectedAt: ISO-8601, source: 'live'|'cache'}` **in directory structure `.oss-preflight/cache/{ecosystem}/{canonical-id}.json` (e.g., `.oss-preflight/cache/npm/discord.js.json`)**. TTLs: npm 6h, GitHub 2h, OpenSSF 24h, discovery 1h. Every call cached including errors (`error: true` marker).
194 | 5. Collector error class carries `ecosystem`, `packageName`, `originalError`, optional `fallbackData`.
195 | 6. **Cache-fallback test passes:** mock GitHub rate-limit response; assert collector returns cached data with `source: 'cache-fallback'`; assert no throw.
196 | 7. **404 test passes:** mock npm 404 response; assert `PackageNotFoundError` thrown; assert no null/fake data returned.
197 | 8. **Cache-invalidation test passes:** write cache entry with `collectedAt` > TTL ago; assert next call fetches live and updates cache.
198 | 9. **Prewarm script is idempotent:** `scripts/prewarm-cache.ts` fetches live npm + GitHub data for demo packages (discord.js, discord.py, discordjs/discord.js repo) and writes to `.oss-preflight/cache/`. **Script checks cache timestamps and skips fetch if data is fresh (within TTL).** Run manually before demo; not part of `pnpm test`.
199 | 10. **Committed demo fixtures exist:** `fixtures/demo-packages/npm-discord.js.json` and `fixtures/demo-packages/github-discordjs-discord.js.json` **committed to git** with real snapshot metadata for demo insurance (fallback if live/cache unavailable).
200 | 11. **PyPI collector (binary):** `pypi.ts` exists and passes unit tests with mocked fetch OR `fixtures/demo-packages/pypi-*.json` fixture exists with documented fallback path. No time-box; either ships or degrades to fixture.
201 | 12. **OpenSSF collector (binary):** `openssf.ts` exists and passes unit tests with mocked fetch OR fixture fallback documented. Missing score â†’ `null`, not failure. No time-box; either ships or degrades to fixture.

203 | **Quality gates** (enforcer named)
204 | - Evidence discipline (no invented facts, explicit nulls) â†’ [`.bob/rules/01-evidence-discipline.md`](../.bob/rules/01-evidence-discipline.md) + [`evidence-discipline`](../.bob/skills/evidence-discipline/SKILL.md) skill
205 | - Engineering standards (security: no secrets logged, cache external calls, parallelize I/O) â†’ [`.bob/rules/02-engineering-standards.md`](../.bob/rules/02-engineering-standards.md)
206 | - Scope binding (no live APIs in unit tests) â†’ [`.bob/rules-code/01-build-floor.md`](../.bob/rules-code/01-build-floor.md)
207 | - Review depth â†’ [`code-review`](../.bob/skills/code-review/SKILL.md) skill
208 | - Test execution â†’ [`test-runner`](../.bob/skills/test-runner/SKILL.md) skill
209 | 
210 | **Test scenarios** (explicit cases, must-test list)
211 | 1. **Cache fallback:** mock GitHub rate-limit; assert returns cached data with `source: 'cache-fallback'`.
212 | 2. **404 handling:** mock npm 404; assert throws `PackageNotFoundError`; assert no null/fake data.
213 | 3. **Cache invalidation:** cache entry older than TTL; assert live fetch + cache update.
214 | 4. **Missing evidence (OpenSSF unavailable):** mock OpenSSF 503; assert returns `null` for score field, does not crash.
215 | 5. **Fixture fallback:** load `fixtures/demo-packages/npm-discord.js.json`; assert valid `license`, `version`, `weeklyDownloads`, `source` URL, `collectedAt`.
216 | 6. **Fixture fallback (GitHub):** load `fixtures/demo-packages/github-discordjs-discord.js.json`; assert valid `stars`, `lastCommit`, `contributors`, `source` URL.
217 | 7. **Error caching:** mock npm timeout; assert error cached with `error: true` marker; second call returns cached error, does not retry immediately.
218 | 8. **Parallel fetch:** fetch npm + GitHub for same package; assert both complete; assert no serial blocking.
219 | 
220 | **Integration success** â€” P2 outputs `packages/collectors/` that P3 (CLI) will import to gather evidence during the recommendation pipeline. The prewarm script and committed fixtures ensure P5 (web UI) demo can run live, from cache, or from fixtures with honest labels. The one-pipeline contract is satisfied: collectors are pure I/O modules with no business logic, called only via the CLI.
221 | 
222 | **Loop config**
223 | - **Steps:** SPEC â†’ IMPLEMENT â†’ REVIEW (reviewer: `code-review`, `evidence-discipline`) â†’ TEST (advanced: `test-runner`, `evidence-discipline`) â†’ FIX (conditional) â†’ ENHANCE (conditional) â†’ LOOP GATE (value-gated, conditional â€” clean pass exits to EXPORT; unmet â‡’ scoped re-verify) â†’ EXPORT â†’ HUMAN REVIEW â†’ COMMIT.
224 | - **Delegated mode per step:** SPECâ†’`plan` Â· IMPLEMENTâ†’`code` Â· REVIEWâ†’`reviewer` Â· TESTâ†’`advanced` Â· FIXâ†’`code` Â· ENHANCEâ†’`code` Â· COMMITâ†’`code`.
225 | - **Loop continuation:** no fixed iteration cap, conditionally scoped. The first REVIEW+TEST pass is full (full review + full must-test list). A clean pass â€” every acceptance criterion green, zero reviewer blockers, full must-test green â€” exits straight to EXPORT with FIX and ENHANCE skipped; no re-verification loop runs. An unmet criterion triggers a scoped FIX and re-verification of only the affected criteria + changed-file tests (plus a regression sanity), widening to a full REVIEW+TEST re-run only when a shared/core contract (types, scorer, serializer, CLI boundary, public schema) was touched. Each loop names its measurable delta; escalate only if progress stalls for two consecutive loops or an external decision is required.
226 | - **Human gate:** mandatory before commit.
227 | 
228 | **Evidence artifact** â€” [`bob_sessions/S04-collectors-cache/`](../bob_sessions/S04-collectors-cache/) with task-history markdown + consumption screenshot. Row in [`bob_sessions/build-report.md`](../bob_sessions/build-report.md): `S04 | <timestamp> | code | evidence-discipline, code-review, test-runner | Implement collectors + cache + prewarm | packages/collectors/, fixtures/, scripts/ | pnpm test, prewarm script | bob_sessions/S04-collectors-cache/ | Single source of factual truth | Exported`
229 | 
230 | **Definition of Done** â€” AC 1â€“10 green (blocking); AC 11â€“12 attempted with time-box (non-blocking); `pnpm test` exits 0 (mocked/fixture-only); prewarm script exists; committed demo fixtures exist; cache fallback proven; evidence exported; human approved; committed with Bob-generated message (`feat(collectors): add npm and GitHub collectors with cache`).

248 | **Scope**

255 | **Acceptance criteria** (binary, testable)
256 | 1. `packages/cli/index.ts` exports a Commander program with two commands: `recommend` and `scaffold`.
257 | 2. `oss-preflight recommend --idea "<string>"` runs the full pipeline: parses intent via Claude Haiku adapter (in CLI, not core) with **temperature=0, seed=42** for deterministic output, invokes core discovery (deterministic catalog), gathers evidence via collectors, scores via core scorer, outputs top 3 ranked recommendations. **On Claude API error (network, auth, rate limit), falls back to keyword-based intent parsing** (extracts ecosystem from keywords like "npm", "discord", "bot"; reduced capability but functional).
258 | 3. `oss-preflight recommend --idea "<discord bot idea>" --json` outputs valid JSON matching [`docs/architecture.md`](../docs/architecture.md) Â§13.1 schema: `recommendations` array with `rank`, `score`, `candidate`, `subscores`, `passport` (facts + interpretation), `scaffoldAvailable`, `templateId`.
259 | 4. `oss-preflight recommend --idea "<discord bot idea>"` (table format, default) prints exactly 3 rows with columns: rank, name, score, goal-fit, maintenance, safety. discord.js is rank 1.
260 | 5. `output-formatter.ts` supports `--format table|json|md`. Passport always in JSON; optional in human output.
261 | 6. CLI reads `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` (required, exits 3 if missing) and `GITHUB_TOKEN` (optional, higher rate limits).
262 | 7. `--refresh` flag forces live collector calls, bypassing cache.
263 | 8. **Exit codes correct:** 0 success, 1 collector/API error, 2 user-input error (empty idea), 3 config error (no API key).
264 | 9. **Table output test passes:** mock collectors + mock Claude; assert output is exactly 3 rows; assert discord.js rank 1.
265 | 10. **JSON schema test passes:** mock collectors + mock Claude; assert output parses as valid JSON; assert matches [`docs/architecture.md`](./architecture.md) Â§13.1 schema.
266 | 11. **Exit-code matrix test passes:** test each exit condition (success, collector fail, empty idea, missing key, Claude fail with fallback); assert correct exit code.
267 | 12. **Claude fallback test passes:** mock Claude API error; assert CLI falls back to keyword-based parsing; assert outputs recommendations (may be reduced quality but functional).
268 | 13. **Hour 14 gate criterion:** `oss-preflight recommend --idea "Discord bot that summarizes channel activity"` prints 3 recommendations. If not green by Hour 14, escalate to user for UI-drop decision.

332 | 8. **Known-good scaffold committed:** `examples/discord-summary-bot/` contains a pre-generated, smoke-test-green scaffold **committed to git** as demo fallback.
333 | 9. **Idempotency test passes:** run scaffold generation twice to same output directory; assert second run skips (no overwrite) or produces identical output.
334 | 10. **Variable interpolation test passes:** template contains `{{PACKAGE_NAME}}`; assert generated file contains actual package name (e.g., `discord.js`).

397 | 5. `pages/ScaffoldProgress.tsx` displays file tree of generated scaffold, live smoke test status (running/pass/fail), and adoption report content.

399 | 7. `server.ts` (Express) exposes `POST /api/recommend` (spawns `oss-preflight recommend --json`, parses stdout, returns `{recommendations, error?}`) and `POST /api/scaffold` (spawns `oss-preflight scaffold`, returns `{files, passed, output}`). **On CLI spawn failure (ENOENT, permission error), returns error response with manual CLI command to run.** No business logic in server â€” thin bridge only.
400 | 8. `components/ScoreBar.tsx` renders a 0â€“100 score as a horizontal bar with color gradient (green high, yellow mid, red low).
401 | 9. `components/FactBadge.tsx` renders a fact with its source link and `(live)` or `(cached)` label.
402 | 10. `components/SourceLink.tsx` renders a clickable source URL with icon.
403 | 11. Dark mode via `class="dark"`; respects `prefers-reduced-motion`; calm mode via `[data-calm=true]`.
404 | 12. **Automated browser test passes:** full flow completes in automated browser test (Playwright or Puppeteer): idea input â†’ submit â†’ 3 cards render â†’ click Passport â†’ modal opens â†’ click Scaffold â†’ files render. No manual verification required.
405 | 13. **CLI spawn failure test passes:** mock CLI spawn failure (ENOENT); assert server returns error response with manual CLI command; assert UI displays error with command.
406 | 14. **API integration test passes:** mock CLI spawn; assert `POST /api/recommend` returns valid JSON; assert `POST /api/scaffold` returns file list.

431 | **Loop config**
432 | - **Steps:** SPEC â†’ IMPLEMENT â†’ REVIEW (reviewer: `code-review`, `evidence-discipline`) â†’ TEST (advanced: `test-runner`, `evidence-discipline`) â†’ FIX (conditional) â†’ ENHANCE (conditional; code for app logic, advanced with `doc-writer` skill for build-proof copy) â†’ LOOP GATE (value-gated, conditional â€” clean pass exits to EXPORT; unmet â‡’ scoped re-verify) â†’ EXPORT â†’ HUMAN REVIEW â†’ COMMIT.
433 | - **Delegated mode per step:** SPECâ†’`plan` Â· IMPLEMENTâ†’`code` Â· REVIEWâ†’`reviewer` Â· TESTâ†’`advanced` Â· FIXâ†’`code` Â· ENHANCEâ†’`code` (app logic), `advanced` (`doc-writer` for build-proof copy) Â· COMMITâ†’`code`.
434 | - **Loop continuation:** no fixed iteration cap, conditionally scoped. The first REVIEW+TEST pass is full (full review + full must-test list). A clean pass â€” every acceptance criterion green, zero reviewer blockers, full must-test green â€” exits straight to EXPORT with FIX and ENHANCE skipped; no re-verification loop runs. An unmet criterion triggers a scoped FIX and re-verification of only the affected criteria + changed-file tests (plus a regression sanity), widening to a full REVIEW+TEST re-run only when a shared/core contract (types, scorer, serializer, CLI boundary, public schema) was touched. Each loop names its measurable delta; escalate only if progress stalls for two consecutive loops or an external decision is required.
435 | - **Human gate:** mandatory before commit.

443 | ## Phase P6 â€” Bob Runtime Integration (maps to session S07)
444 | 
445 | **Objective** â€” Prove OSS Preflight also ships as a Bob workflow by implementing and demonstrating the `oss-preflight-advisor` skill activation in Advanced mode, presenting recommendations (or the exact CLI sequence), and respecting the sandboxed `oss-preflight-scaffolder` mode's approved-path fence.

Success is measured by: skill activates in Advanced mode (guaranteed runtime per [`docs/bob-build-guide.md`](../docs/bob-build-guide.md) Â§2); presents top recommendation with Evidence Passport summary; asks before scaffolding; writes only to approved paths ([`.oss-preflight/`, `docs/oss-preflight/`, `examples/`, `oss-preflight-output/`]).

456 | 
457 | **Scope**
458 | - **In:** finish/test `oss-preflight-advisor` skill (reads repo context, runs CLI or states the exact command sequence, presents top recommendation, asks before scaffolding); test `oss-preflight-scaffolder` mode fence (writes only to approved paths); record 30-second activation clip (optional fallback if live demo risky).

461 | 
462 | **Preconditions** â€” P3 and P4 complete and committed: `packages/cli/` exports `recommend` and `scaffold` commands working; `oss-preflight recommend` prints 3 recommendations; `oss-preflight scaffold` produces files with green smoke test.
463 | 
464 | **Acceptance criteria** (binary, testable)
465 | 1. `.bob/skills/oss-preflight-advisor/SKILL.md` exists with `name: oss-preflight-advisor` and `description` containing explicit keyword triggers: "run OSS Preflight", "oss-preflight", "package recommendation", "stack recommendation", "OSS starter".
466 | 2. **Skill activates on keyword match:** open Advanced mode; say "Run OSS Preflight on this idea: Discord bot that summarizes channel activity"; assert skill activates (exact keyword match, no LLM interpretation).
467 | 3. **Skill reads repo context:** skill inspects `package.json`, `README.md`, language, framework, test command (if available).
468 | 4. **Skill presents CLI sequence or runs it:** skill either runs `oss-preflight recommend --idea "<idea>"` or states the exact command for the user to run. If CLI not available, states the intended command and stops.
469 | 5. **Skill presents top recommendation:** displays rank 1 recommendation with score, Evidence Passport summary (facts vs interpretation), missing-evidence notes, tradeoffs.
470 | 6. **Skill asks before scaffolding:** after presenting recommendations, asks "Scaffold the top option?" and waits for approval. Never writes without approval.
471 | 7. **Scaffolder mode fence holds:** if user approves scaffold, skill switches to `oss-preflight-scaffolder` mode or delegates to it; assert writes only to `.oss-preflight/`, `docs/oss-preflight/`, `examples/`, `oss-preflight-output/`. Attempt to write to `src/` or `packages/` is blocked by `fileRegex`.
472 | 8. **Fence test passes (blocked paths):** in `oss-preflight-scaffolder` mode, attempt to write to each: `src/app.ts`, `packages/core/types.ts`, `apps/web/App.tsx`, `.bob/custom_modes.yaml`; assert all blocked with `FileRestrictionError`.
473 | 9. **Fence test passes (approved paths):** in `oss-preflight-scaffolder` mode, write to each: `.oss-preflight/test.md`, `docs/oss-preflight/guide.md`, `examples/my-scaffold/index.ts`, `oss-preflight-output/report.json`; assert all succeed.
474 | 10. **Fence test passes (edge cases):** attempt to write to `.oss-preflight/../src/app.ts` (path traversal); assert blocked. Attempt to write to `examples/` (directory, not file); assert succeeds.
475 | 11. **(Optional) Activation clip recorded:** 30-second screen recording showing skill activation, recommendation presentation, and fence respect. Fallback if live demo risky.

581 | This phase-plan document is now complete. Every phase (P1â€“P7) implements the full [`docs/bob-prompts.md`](./bob-prompts.md) Â§4 contract with zero omissions and zero open questions. Each specification is self-contained and Orchestrator-ready.

431 | **Loop config**
432 | - **Steps:** SPEC â†’ IMPLEMENT â†’ REVIEW (reviewer: `code-review`, `evidence-discipline`) â†’ TEST (advanced: `test-runner`, `evidence-discipline`) â†’ FIX (conditional) â†’ ENHANCE (conditional; code for app logic, advanced with `doc-writer` skill for build-proof copy) â†’ LOOP GATE (value-gated, conditional â€” clean pass exits to EXPORT; unmet â‡’ scoped re-verify) â†’ EXPORT â†’ HUMAN REVIEW â†’ COMMIT.
433 | - **Delegated mode per step:** SPECâ†’`plan` Â· IMPLEMENTâ†’`code` Â· REVIEWâ†’`reviewer` Â· TESTâ†’`advanced` Â· FIXâ†’`code` Â· ENHANCEâ†’`code` (app logic), `advanced` (`doc-writer` for build-proof copy) Â· COMMITâ†’`code`.
434 | - **Loop continuation:** no fixed iteration cap, conditionally scoped. The first REVIEW+TEST pass is full (full review + full must-test list). A clean pass â€” every acceptance criterion green, zero reviewer blockers, full must-test green â€” exits straight to EXPORT with FIX and ENHANCE skipped; no re-verification loop runs. An unmet criterion triggers a scoped FIX and re-verification of only the affected criteria + changed-file tests (plus a regression sanity), widening to a full REVIEW+TEST re-run only when a shared/core contract (types, scorer, serializer, CLI boundary, public schema) was touched. Each loop names its measurable delta; escalate only if progress stalls for two consecutive loops or an external decision is required.

 1 | #!/usr/bin/env node
 2 | 
 3 | /**
 4 |  * OSS Preflight CLI - Phase P3
 5 |  * 
 6 |  * Main entry point with Commander.js setup
 7 |  * Two commands: recommend and scaffold
 8 |  * 
 9 |  * One-pipeline contract: web and skill call this CLI, never import core directly
10 |  */
11 | 
12 | import { Command } from 'commander';
13 | import { runRecommendPipeline, checkEnvironment, validateInput } from './recommend-command.js';
14 | import { scaffoldCommand } from './scaffold-command.js';
15 | import { formatOutput } from './output-formatter.js';
16 | 
17 | const program = new Command();
18 | 
19 | program
20 |   .name('oss-preflight')
21 |   .description('OSS Preflight - Evidence-backed package recommendations')
22 |   .version('0.1.0');
23 | 
24 | /**
25 |  * Recommend command - full pipeline
26 |  */
27 | program
28 |   .command('recommend')
29 |   .description('Get package recommendations for your idea')
30 |   .requiredOption('--idea <string>', 'Your software idea or requirement')
31 |   .option('--json', 'Output as JSON')
32 |   .option('--format <type>', 'Output format: table, json, or md', 'table')
33 |   .option('--refresh', 'Force live collector calls, bypass cache')
34 |   .action(async (options) => {
35 |     try {
36 |       // Validate environment
37 |       checkEnvironment();
38 |       
39 |       // Validate input
40 |       validateInput(options.idea);
41 |       
42 |       // Run pipeline
43 |       const { recommendations, brief } = await runRecommendPipeline(options.idea, {
44 |         refresh: options.refresh
45 |       });
46 |       
47 |       // Determine format
48 |       const format = options.json ? 'json' : (options.format || 'table');
49 |       
50 |       // Format and output
51 |       const output = formatOutput(recommendations, brief, format as 'table' | 'json' | 'md');
52 |       console.log(output);
53 |       
54 |       process.exit(0);
55 |     } catch (error) {
56 |       const err = error as Error;
57 |       
58 |       // Exit code logic per architecture.md Â§14
59 |       if (err.message.includes('ANTHROPIC_API_KEY')) {
60 |         console.error('Error: ANTHROPIC_API_KEY environment variable is required');
61 |         process.exit(3); // Config error
62 |       } else if (err.message.includes('empty') || err.message.includes('cannot be empty')) {
63 |         console.error('Error: Idea string cannot be empty');
64 |         process.exit(2); // User input error
65 |       } else {
66 |         console.error('Error:', err.message);
67 |         process.exit(1); // Collector/API error
68 |       }
69 |     }
70 |   });
71 | 
72 | /**
73 |  * Scaffold command - stub for P4
74 |  */
75 | program
76 |   .command('scaffold')
77 |   .description('Generate a working starter from a recommendation (Phase P4)')
78 |   .option('--recommendation <json>', 'Recommendation JSON file or string')
79 |   .option('--out <directory>', 'Output directory for generated code')
80 |   .action(async (options) => {
81 |     await scaffoldCommand(options);
82 |   });
83 | 
84 | // Export for testing
85 | export { program };
86 | 
87 | // Parse arguments only if this is the main module
88 | if (import.meta.url === `file://${process.argv[1]}` || process.argv[1]?.endsWith('index.js')) {
89 |   program.parse();
90 | }

 1 | import type { Recommendation } from '@oss-preflight/core';
 2 | import * as fs from 'fs';
 3 | import * as path from 'path';
 4 | import * as crypto from 'crypto';
 5 | import { fileURLToPath } from 'url';
 6 | import { dirname } from 'path';
 7 | 
 8 | export interface ScaffoldResult {
 9 |   success: boolean;
10 |   skipped: boolean;
11 |   message: string;
12 | }
13 | 
14 | /**
15 |  * Generate a version hash for idempotency check
16 |  */
17 | function generateVersionHash(recommendation: Recommendation): string {
18 |   const hashInput = `${recommendation.candidate.name}@${recommendation.candidate.version}`;
19 |   return crypto.createHash('sha256').update(hashInput).digest('hex').substring(0, 16);
20 | }
21 | 
22 | /**
23 |  * Check if scaffold already exists with matching version hash
24 |  */
25 | function checkIdempotency(outputDir: string, versionHash: string): boolean {
26 |   const hashFile = path.join(outputDir, '.scaffold-version');
27 |   
28 |   if (!fs.existsSync(outputDir)) {
29 |     return false;
30 |   }
31 | 
32 |   if (!fs.existsSync(hashFile)) {
33 |     return false;
34 |   }
35 | 
36 |   const existingHash = fs.readFileSync(hashFile, 'utf-8').trim();
37 |   return existingHash === versionHash;
38 | }
39 | 
40 | /**
41 |  * Interpolate template variables
42 |  */
43 | function interpolateTemplate(content: string, recommendation: Recommendation): string {
44 |   return content
45 |     .replace(/\{\{PACKAGE_NAME\}\}/g, recommendation.candidate.name)
46 |     .replace(/\{\{PACKAGE_VERSION\}\}/g, recommendation.candidate.version)
47 |     .replace(/\{\{REPOSITORY_URL\}\}/g, recommendation.candidate.repositoryUrl || '')
48 |     .replace(/\{\{HOMEPAGE_URL\}\}/g, recommendation.candidate.homepageUrl || '');
49 | }
50 |

# Reminder: Instructions for Tool Use

Tool uses are formatted using XML-style tags. The tool name itself becomes the XML tag name. Each parameter is enclosed within its own set of tags. Here's the structure:

<actual_tool_name>
<parameter1_name>value1</parameter1_name>
<parameter2_name>value2</parameter2_name>
...
</actual_tool_name>

For example, to use the attempt_completion tool:

<attempt_completion>
<result>
I have completed the task...
</result>
</attempt_completion>

Always use the actual tool name as the XML tag name for proper parsing and execution.

<message>STEP 2: IMPLEMENT Phase P5 (Web UI + Build-Proof) per [`docs/phase-plan.md`](docs/phase-plan.md:370-439).

**These instructions supersede any conflicting general mode instructions. Work ONLY to this spec. Do not deviate.**

## Goal (tightly scoped)

Implement the web UI that runs the full idea-to-scaffold flow in the browser and a `/build-proof` page that renders Bob evidence, satisfying all 14 acceptance criteria in the P5 spec.

## Context (self-contained)

- **Architecture:** [`docs/architecture.md`](docs/architecture.md) Â§5 (fact/inference split), Â§6 (system architecture), Â§13.2 (web API: Express bridge spawns CLI), Â§17 (judge success criteria)
- **Implementation plan:** [`docs/implementation-plan.md`](docs/implementation-plan.md) Â§5 P5 (files, notes, tests, exit gate, pro tips), Â§4 timeline (Hour 24 gate), Â§8 (demo script)
- **P3 output:** [`packages/cli/`](packages/cli/) (CLI to spawn with `--json` flag)
- **P4 output:** [`packages/scaffold/`](packages/scaffold/) (scaffold engine)
- **Design tokens:** [`context/ui-reference/oss-preflight-design-tokens.css`](context/ui-reference/oss-preflight-design-tokens.css)
- **Mode fence:** [`.bob/custom_modes.yaml`](..bob/custom_modes.yaml) code mode `fileRegex` permits `apps/`
- **Bob evidence:** [`bob_sessions/build-report.md`](bob_sessions/build-report.md) (to render in `/build-proof`)

## Scope (binding contract)

**IN:**
- `apps/web/` with `src/App.tsx`, `pages/{IdeaInput,RecommendationList,EvidencePassport,ScaffoldProgress,BuildProof}.tsx`, `components/{ScoreBar,FactBadge,SourceLink,HighlightCode}.tsx`, `api/client.ts`, `server.ts` (Express bridge spawning CLI with `--json`)
- Vite + Tailwind config
- Design tokens from [`context/ui-reference/oss-preflight-design-tokens.css`](context/ui-reference/oss-preflight-design-tokens.css)
- Lightweight component snapshots (optional)
- API integration test against mock CLI

**OUT (cutline):**
- Repo flow (drop if Hour 24 gate fails)
- GitHub starter search
- Live repo analysis
- Component library
- Heavy state lib (use Context + hooks only)
- PyPI/OpenSSF/Hugging Face (unless P2 shipped them)
- Bob skill integration (P6)
- Advanced similarity scoring

## Acceptance Criteria (14 binary, testable â€” ALL must be green)

1. `apps/web/src/App.tsx` renders the main flow: idea input â†’ recommendation list â†’ Evidence Passport modal â†’ scaffold progress â†’ build-proof page
2. `pages/IdeaInput.tsx` accepts a text input (idea string) and a submit button; on submit, calls `POST /api/recommend` with the idea
3. `pages/RecommendationList.tsx` displays exactly 3 recommendation cards with rank, name, score, goal-fit, maintenance, safety. Each card has an "Open Passport" button
4. `pages/EvidencePassport.tsx` (modal) displays the selected recommendation's passport with **two visibly separated columns:** Facts (sourced, with source URLs, collectedAt timestamps, sourceType labels) and Interpretation (AI-derived: goal-fit summary, compatibility narrative, tradeoffs, warnings). Missing fields show `(not available)`
5. `pages/ScaffoldProgress.tsx` displays file tree of generated scaffold, live smoke test status (running/pass/fail), and adoption report content
6. `pages/BuildProof.tsx` (or `/build-proof` route) renders Bob evidence: `.bob/custom_modes.yaml` summary, `.bob/skills/` list, `bob_sessions/` export list with links, `bob_sessions/build-report.md` content, git log showing Bob-assisted commits
7. `server.ts` (Express) exposes `POST /api/recommend` (spawns `oss-preflight recommend --json`, parses stdout, returns `{recommendations, error?}`) and `POST /api/scaffold` (spawns `oss-preflight scaffold`, returns `{files, passed, output}`). **On CLI spawn failure (ENOENT, permission error), returns error response with manual CLI command to run.** No business logic in server â€” thin bridge only
8. `components/ScoreBar.tsx` renders a 0â€“100 score as a horizontal bar with color gradient (green high, yellow mid, red low)
9. `components/FactBadge.tsx` renders a fact with its source link and `(live)` or `(cached)` label
10. `components/SourceLink.tsx` renders a clickable source URL with icon
11. Dark mode via `class="dark"`; respects `prefers-reduced-motion`; calm mode via `[data-calm=true]`
12. **Automated browser test passes:** full flow completes in automated browser test (Playwright or Puppeteer): idea input â†’ submit â†’ 3 cards render â†’ click Passport â†’ modal opens â†’ click Scaffold â†’ files render. No manual verification required
13. **CLI spawn failure test passes:** mock CLI spawn failure (ENOENT); assert server returns error response with manual CLI command; assert UI displays error with command
14. **API integration test passes:** mock CLI spawn; assert `POST /api/recommend` returns valid JSON; assert `POST /api/scaffold` returns file list

## Quality Gates (enforcers â€” will be checked in REVIEW/TEST)

- Evidence discipline (fact/inference split visible, missing evidence explicit) â†’ [`.bob/rules/01-evidence-discipline.md`](.bob/rules/01-evidence-discipline.md)
- Engineering standards (one pipeline: server spawns CLI, never imports core) â†’ [`.bob/rules/02-engineering-standards.md`](.bob/rules/02-engineering-standards.md)
- Scope binding â†’ [`.bob/rules/03-scope-and-gates.md`](.bob/rules/03-scope-and-gates.md) (Hour 24 gate)

## Instructions

1. **Bootstrap `apps/web/` package:** Create `package.json`, `vite.config.ts`, `tailwind.config.js`, `tsconfig.json`
2. **Implement pages:** `IdeaInput.tsx`, `RecommendationList.tsx`, `EvidencePassport.tsx`, `ScaffoldProgress.tsx`, `BuildProof.tsx`
3. **Implement components:** `ScoreBar.tsx`, `FactBadge.tsx`, `SourceLink.tsx`, `HighlightCode.tsx`
4. **Implement API client:** `api/client.ts` (fetch wrappers for `/api/recommend` and `/api/scaffold`)
5. **Implement Express server:** `server.ts` (spawns CLI, handles errors, returns JSON)

8. **Write tests:** API integration test (mock CLI spawn), CLI spawn failure test, automated browser test (Playwright/Puppeteer)
9. **Verify all 14 AC:** Check each criterion is met

## Acceptance Criteria (14 binary, testable â€” ALL must be green)

1. `apps/web/src/App.tsx` renders the main flow: idea input â†’ recommendation list â†’ Evidence Passport modal â†’ scaffold progress â†’ build-proof page
2. `pages/IdeaInput.tsx` accepts a text input (idea string) and a submit button; on submit, calls `POST /api/recommend` with the idea
3. `pages/RecommendationList.tsx` displays exactly 3 recommendation cards with rank, name, score, goal-fit, maintenance, safety. Each card has an "Open Passport" button
4. `pages/EvidencePassport.tsx` (modal) displays the selected recommendation's passport with **two visibly separated columns:** Facts (sourced, with source URLs, collectedAt timestamps, sourceType labels) and Interpretation (AI-derived: goal-fit summary, compatibility narrative, tradeoffs, warnings). Missing fields show `(not available)`
5. `pages/ScaffoldProgress.tsx` displays file tree of generated scaffold, live smoke test status (running/pass/fail), and adoption report content
6. `pages/BuildProof.tsx` (or `/build-proof` route) renders Bob evidence: `.bob/custom_modes.yaml` summary, `.bob/skills/` list, `bob_sessions/` export list with links, `bob_sessions/build-report.md` content, git log showing Bob-assisted commits
7. `server.ts` (Express) exposes `POST /api/recommend` (spawns `oss-preflight recommend --json`, parses stdout, returns `{recommendations, error?}`) and `POST /api/scaffold` (spawns `oss-preflight scaffold`, returns `{files, passed, output}`). **On CLI spawn failure (ENOENT, permission error), returns error response with manual CLI command to run.** No business logic in server â€” thin bridge only
8. `components/ScoreBar.tsx` renders a 0â€“100 score as a horizontal bar with color gradient (green high, yellow mid, red low)
9. `components/FactBadge.tsx` renders a fact with its source link and `(live)` or `(cached)` label
10. `components/SourceLink.tsx` renders a clickable source URL with icon
11. Dark mode via `class="dark"`; respects `prefers-reduced-motion`; calm mode via `[data-calm=true]`
12. **Automated browser test passes:** full flow completes in automated browser test (Playwright or Puppeteer): idea input â†’ submit â†’ 3 cards render â†’ click Passport â†’ modal opens â†’ click Scaffold â†’ files render. No manual verification required
13. **CLI spawn failure test passes:** mock CLI spawn failure (ENOENT); assert server returns error response with manual CLI command; assert UI displays error with command
14. **API integration test passes:** mock CLI spawn; assert `POST /api/recommend` returns valid JSON; assert `POST /api/scaffold` returns file list

**User:**

[new_task completed] Result: # P5 (Web UI + Build-Proof) Review â€” VERDICT: **1 BLOCKER FOUND**

## BLOCKERS (must fix before TEST)

### BLOCKER 1: Engineering Standards Violation â€” Server Imports Core Directly
**Location:** [`apps/web/server.ts:29`](apps/web/server.ts:29)
**Violation:** AC7 requires "No business logic in server â€” thin bridge only" and engineering standards mandate "one pipeline: server spawns CLI, never imports core"
**Issue:** Server directly spawns `tsx` with the CLI source path (`packages/cli/src/index.ts`) instead of spawning the installed `oss-preflight` CLI command. This violates the one-pipeline contract.
**Impact:** The web server is not using the same execution path as the CLI. This breaks the demo requirement that "the demo path is the same as the CLI path."
**Fix Required:** Change spawn command from `tsx [cliPath]` to `oss-preflight` (the installed CLI binary), ensuring the server uses the published CLI interface, not internal source files.

---

## ACCEPTANCE CRITERIA STATUS (14 total)

âś… **AC1:** App.tsx renders main flow (idea â†’ recommendations â†’ passport modal â†’ scaffold â†’ build-proof) â€” PASS
âś… **AC2:** IdeaInput accepts text input and submit, calls POST /api/recommend â€” PASS
âś… **AC3:** RecommendationList displays 3 cards with rank, name, score, subscores, "Open Passport" button â€” PASS
âś… **AC4:** EvidencePassport displays two visibly separated columns (Facts with sources | Interpretation AI-derived), missing fields show "(not available)" â€” PASS
âś… **AC5:** ScaffoldProgress displays file tree, smoke test status (running/pass/fail), adoption report â€” PASS
âś… **AC6:** BuildProof renders Bob evidence (.bob/custom_modes.yaml summary, skills list, bob_sessions/ exports, build-report.md, git log) â€” PASS
âťŚ **AC7:** Server spawns CLI with error handling â€” **BLOCKER** (spawns source files via tsx, not installed CLI)
âś… **AC8:** ScoreBar renders 0-100 score with color gradient (green high, yellow mid, red low) â€” PASS
âś… **AC9:** FactBadge renders fact with source link and (live)/(cached) label â€” PASS
âś… **AC10:** SourceLink renders clickable source URL with icon â€” PASS
âś… **AC11:** Dark mode via class="dark", respects prefers-reduced-motion, calm mode via data-calm â€” PASS
âś… **AC12:** Automated browser test passes (full flow in Playwright) â€” PASS (test exists and covers flow)
âś… **AC13:** CLI spawn failure test passes (mock ENOENT, assert error response with manual command) â€” PASS
âś… **AC14:** API integration test passes (mock CLI spawn, assert valid JSON responses) â€” PASS

**Score: 13/14 AC green, 1 blocker**

---

## QUALITY FINDINGS (non-blocking, for ENHANCE)

### 1. Test Coverage Gaps
- **Location:** [`apps/web/__tests__/server.test.ts`](apps/web/__tests__/server.test.ts:1-91)
- **Issue:** Server tests mock the error handling logic but don't actually test the Express server endpoints with real spawn failures
- **Recommendation:** Add integration tests that start the Express server and mock `child_process.spawn` to verify actual HTTP error responses

### 2. BuildProof Static Content
- **Location:** [`apps/web/src/pages/BuildProof.tsx:16-26`](apps/web/src/pages/BuildProof.tsx:16-26)
- **Issue:** BuildProof attempts to fetch `/bob_sessions/build-report.md` but this won't work in production without serving static files
- **Recommendation:** Add Express static file serving for `bob_sessions/` directory or fetch via API endpoint

### 3. Hardcoded Git Log
- **Location:** [`apps/web/src/pages/BuildProof.tsx:142-183`](apps/web/src/pages/BuildProof.tsx:142-183)
- **Issue:** Git log is hardcoded placeholder data instead of fetched from actual git history
- **Recommendation:** Add API endpoint to fetch real git log or document this as demo data

### 4. Missing Test Scenarios
- **Missing:** Test scenario #4 (missing evidence shows "(not available)") not explicitly tested
- **Missing:** Test scenario #10 (dark mode toggle) exists but #11 (calm mode) not tested
- **Recommendation:** Add explicit tests for these scenarios in the test suite

- âś… Facts column clearly separated from Interpretation column in EvidencePassport
- âś… Missing evidence explicitly shown as "(not available)" in FactBadge and EvidencePassport
- âś… Source URLs, timestamps, and sourceType labels present in FactBadge
- âś… No invented package facts in UI code

- âś… No repo flow implemented (correctly cut per spec line 388)
- âś… All features within P5 scope
- âś… No features beyond spec

<message>STEP 5: FIX BLOCKER 1 from P5 REVIEW.

**These instructions supersede any conflicting general mode instructions. Fix ONLY this blocker. Do not deviate.**

## Blocker to Fix

**BLOCKER 1: Engineering Standards Violation â€” Server Imports Core Directly**
- **Location:** [`apps/web/server.ts:29`](apps/web/server.ts:29) and [`apps/web/server.ts:102-108`](apps/web/server.ts:102-108)
- **Violation:** AC7 requires "No business logic in server â€” thin bridge only" and engineering standards mandate "one pipeline: server spawns CLI, never imports core"
- **Issue:** Server directly spawns `tsx` with the CLI source path (`packages/cli/src/index.ts`) instead of spawning the installed `oss-preflight` CLI command. This violates the one-pipeline contract.
- **Impact:** The web server is not using the same execution path as the CLI. This breaks the demo requirement that "the demo path is the same as the CLI path."

## Fix Required

Change spawn commands in [`apps/web/server.ts`](apps/web/server.ts) from:
```typescript
spawn('tsx', [cliPath, 'recommend', '--idea', idea, '--json'])
```

To:
```typescript
spawn('oss-preflight', ['recommend', '--idea', idea, '--json'])
```

And from:
```typescript
spawn('tsx', [cliPath, 'scaffold', '--recommendation', ...])
```

To:
```typescript
spawn('oss-preflight', ['scaffold', '--recommendation', ...])
```

## Instructions

1. Read [`apps/web/server.ts`](apps/web/server.ts)
2. Locate the two spawn calls (lines ~29 and ~102-108)
3. Replace `tsx` + `cliPath` with `oss-preflight` (the installed CLI binary)
4. Remove the `cliPath` variable and path resolution logic (no longer needed)
5. Verify the spawn commands now use the published CLI interface
6. Use attempt_completion to confirm the fix

**Fix ONLY this blocker. Do not make other changes.**</message>
</new_task>

---

**User:**

[new_task completed] Result: **BLOCKER 1 FIXED: Server Now Uses Installed CLI Binary**

Changed `apps/web/server.ts` to spawn the installed `oss-preflight` CLI command instead of directly executing the source with `tsx`:

**Line 29 (recommend endpoint):**
- Before: `spawn('tsx', [cliPath, 'recommend', '--idea', idea, '--json'])`
- After: `spawn('oss-preflight', ['recommend', '--idea', idea, '--json'])`

**Line 103 (scaffold endpoint):**
- Before: `spawn('tsx', [cliPath, 'scaffold', '--recommendation', tempFile, '--out', outputDir])`
- After: `spawn('oss-preflight', ['scaffold', '--recommendation', tempFile, '--out', outputDir])`

**Removed:**
- `cliPath` variable and path resolution logic (no longer needed)

The server now correctly implements the one-pipeline contract: web â†’ CLI â†’ core (never web â†’ core directly). This satisfies AC7 "No business logic in server â€” thin bridge only" and the engineering standard that "server spawns CLI, never imports core."
